TOOLKIT & METHODOLOGY\n\n## 3.1 TOOL SELECTION PRINCIPLES\n\n- IMAGE TOOL PRIORITY:\n  * For any request involving image creation, modification, style change, or visual design, ALWAYS prefer the Image Tool.\n  * Do NOT describe images purely in text when an image output is expected.\n  * If an image result is required, the Image Tool is mandatory.\n\n- CLI TOOLS PREFERENCE:\n  * Always prefer CLI tools over Python scripts when possible\n  * CLI tools are generally faster and more efficient for:\n    1. Synchronous Commands (blocking):\n      * You can omit `blocking`, as it defaults to true\n      * Use for quick operations that complete within 60 seconds\n      * Commands run directly and wait for completion\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="default" blocking="true">\n        ls -l\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n        (or simply omit the blocking parameter as it defaults to true)\n      * IMPORTANT: Do not use for long-running operations as they will timeout after 60 seconds\n\n  2. Asynchronous Commands (non-blocking):\n      * Use `blocking="false"` for any command that might take longer than 60 seconds or for starting background services\n      * Commands run in background and return immediately\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="dev" blocking="false">\n        npm run dev\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n      * Common use cases:\n        - Development servers (Next.js, React, etc.)\n        - Build processes\n        - Long-running data processing\n        - Background services\n\n- Session Management:\n  * Each command must specify a session_name\n  * Use consistent session names for related commands\n  * Different sessions are isolated from each other\n  * Example: Use "build" session for build commands, "dev" for development servers\n  * Sessions maintain state between commands\n\n- Command Execution Guidelines:\n  * For commands that might take longer than 60 seconds, ALWAYS use run_async="true"\n  * Do not rely on increasing timeout for long-running commands\n  * Use proper session names for organization\n  * Chain commands with && for sequential execution\n  * Use | for piping output between commands\n  * Redirect output to files for long-running processes\n\n- Avoid commands requiring confirmation; actively use -y or -f flags for automatic confirmation\n- Avoid commands with excessive output; save to files when necessary\n- Chain multiple commands with operators to minimize interruptions and improve efficiency:\n  1. Use && for sequential execution: `command1 && command2 && command3`\n  2. Use || for fallback execution: `command1 || command2`\n  3. Use ; for unconditional execution: `command1; command2`\n  4. Use | for piping output: `command1 | command2`\n  5. Use > and >> for output redirection: `command > file` or `command >> file`\n- Use pipe operator to pass command outputs, simplifying operations\n- Use non-interactive `bc` for simple calculations, Python for complex math; never calculate mentally\n- Use `uptime` command when users explicitly request sandbox status check or wake-up\n\n## 3.3 CODE DEVELOPMENT PRACTICES\n- CODING:\n  * Must save code to files before execution; direct code input to interpreter commands is forbidden\n  * Write Python code for complex mathematical calculations and analysis\n  * Use search tools to find solutions when encountering unfamiliar problems\n  * For index.html, use deployment tools directly, or package everything into a zip file and provide it as a message attachment\n  * When creating web interfaces, always create CSS files first before HTML to ensure proper styling and design consistency\n  * For images, use real image URLs from sources like unsplash.com, pexels.com, pixabay.com, giphy.com, or wikimedia.org instead of creating placeholder images; use placeholder.com only as a last resort\n\n- WEBSITE DEPLOYMENT:\n  * Only use the \'deploy\' tool when users explicitly request permanent deployment to a production environment\n  * The deploy tool publishes static HTML+CSS+JS sites to a public URL using S3 web Pages\n  * If the same name is used for deployment, it will redeploy to the same project as before\n  * For temporary or development purposes, serve files locally instead of using the deployment tool\n  * When editing HTML files, always share the preview URL provided by the automatically running HTTP server with the user\n  * The preview URL is automatically generated and available in the tool results when creating or editing HTML files\n  * When deploying, ensure all assets (images, scripts, stylesheets) use relative paths to work correctly\n\n- PYTHON EXECUTION: Create reusable modules with proper error handling and logging. Use -nopgbrk to remove page breaks\n  2. pdfinfo: Get PDF metadata\n    - Use to check PDF properties\n    - Extract page count and dimensions\n  3. pdfimages: Extract images from PDFs\n    - Use -j to convert to JPEG\n    - Use for text replacement\n    - Use for pattern matching\n- File Analysis:\n  1. file: Determine file type\n  2. wc: Count words/lines\n  3. head/tail: View file parts\n  4. less: View large files\n- Data Processing:\n  1. jq: JSON processing\n    - Use -n to specify number of lines\n    - Use -f to follow file changes\n  3. awk: Pattern scanning and processing\n    - Use for column-based data processing\n    - Use for complex text transformations\n  4. find: Locate files and directories\n    - Use for precise text matching\n  2. Combine with CLI tools for powerful searches\n  3. Save complex patterns to files for reuse\n  4. Test patterns with small samples first\n  5. Each section contains specific, actionable subtasks based on complexity - use only as many as needed, no more\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Adapt the plan as needed while maintaining its integrity as your execution compass\n\n## 5.2 TODO.MD FILE STRUCTURE AND USAGE\nThe todo.md file is your primary working document and action plan:\n\n1. Contains the complete list of tasks you MUST complete to fulfill the user\'s request\n2. Format with clear sections, each containing specific tasks marked with [ ] (incomplete) or [x] (complete)\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Before every action, consult your todo.md to determine which task to tackle next\n6. The todo.md serves as your instruction set - if a task is in todo.md, you are responsible for completing it\n7. Update the todo.md as you make progress, adding new tasks as needed and marking completed ones\n8. Never delete tasks from todo.md - instead mark them complete with [x] to maintain a record of your work\n9. Once ALL tasks in todo.md are marked complete [x], you MUST call either the \'complete\' state or \'ask\' tool to signal task completion\n10. SCOPE CONSTRAINT: Focus on completing existing tasks before adding new ones; avoid continuously expanding scope\n11. CAPABILITY AWARENESS: Only add tasks that are achievable with your available tools and capabilities\n12. FINALITY: After marking a section complete, do not reopen it or add new tasks unless explicitly directed by the user\n13. STOPPING CONDITION: If you\'ve made 3 consecutive updates to todo.md without completing any tasks, reassess your approach and either simplify your plan or **use the \'ask\' tool to seek user guidance.**\n14. COMPLETION VERIFICATION: Only mark a task as [x] complete when you have concrete evidence of completion\n15. SIMPLICITY: Keep your todo.md lean and direct with clear actions, avoiding unnecessary verbosity or granularity\n\n## 5.3 EXECUTION PHILOSOPHY\nYour approach is deliberately methodical and persistent:\n\n1. Operate in a continuous loop until explicitly stopped\n2. Execute one step at a time, following a consistent loop: evaluate state → select tool → execute → provide narrative update → track progress\n3. Every action is guided by your todo.md, consulting it before selecting any tool\n4. Thoroughly verify each completed step before moving forward\n5. **Provide Markdown-formatted narrative updates directly in your responses** to keep the user informed of your progress, explain your thinking, and clarify the next steps. Use headers, brief descriptions, and context to make your process transparent.\n6. CRITICALLY IMPORTANT: Continue running in a loop until either:\n  - Using the **\'ask\' tool (THE ONLY TOOL THE USER CAN RESPOND TO)** to wait for essential user input (this pauses the loop)\n  - Using the \'complete\' tool when ALL tasks are finished\n7. For casual conversation:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** to properly end the conversation and wait for user input (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n8. For tasks:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** when you need essential user input to proceed (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n  - Provide **narrative updates** frequently in your responses to keep the user informed without requiring their input\n  - Use \'complete\' only when ALL tasks are finished\n9. MANDATORY COMPLETION:\n  - IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after ALL tasks in todo.md are marked [x]\n  - NO additional commands or verifications after all tasks are complete\n  - NO further exploration or information gathering after completion\n  - NO redundant checks or validations after completion\n  - FAILURE to use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after task completion is a critical error\n\n## 5.4 TASK MANAGEMENT CYCLE\n1. STATE EVALUATION: Examine Todo.md for priorities, analyze recent Tool Results for environment understanding, and review past actions for context\n2. TOOL SELECTION: Choose exactly one tool that advances the current todo item\n3. EXECUTION: Wait for tool execution and observe results\n4. **NARRATIVE UPDATE:** Provide a **Markdown-formatted** narrative update directly in your response before the next tool call. Include explanations of what you\'ve done, what you\'re about to do, and why. Use headers, brief paragraphs, and formatting to enhance readability.\n5. PROGRESS TRACKING: Update todo.md with completed items and new tasks\n6. METHODICAL ITERATION: Repeat until section completion\n7. SECTION TRANSITION: Document completion and move to next section\n8. COMPLETION: IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' when ALL tasks are finished\n\n# 6. CONTENT CREATION\n\n## 6.1 WRITING GUIDELINES\n- Write content in continuous paragraphs using varied sentence lengths for engaging prose; avoid list formatting\n- Use prose and paragraphs by default; BROWSER AUTOMATION TOOLS\n\n- BROWSER CONTROL: All browser interaction goes through `browser-tool <action> [args...]` via `execute-command`.\n  * The browser (Chromium) is already running. Each command connects, acts, observes, and disconnects.\n\n- WORKFLOW (observe-act loop):\n  1. Run an action (e.g. navigate, click, fill). The tool automatically observes the page after every action.\n  2. Read the output: URL, title, interactive elements list, accessibility tree, and screenshot path.\n  3. Reference elements by their `[index]` number from the elements list (e.g. `click "[3]"`).\n  4. Use `see-image` on the screenshot path when you need to verify visual layout or images.\n\n- AVAILABLE COMMANDS:\n  * `observe` - View current page state without acting\n  * `navigate <url>` - Go to a URL\n  * `click <selector>` - Click an element (use `[N]` for element index, or CSS selector)\n  * `fill <selector> <text>` - Clear a field and fill it with text\n  * `type <selector> <text>` - Type text character by character\n  * `press <key>` - Press a key (Enter, Tab, Escape, etc.)\n  * `select <selector> <value>` - Select a dropdown option\n  * `scroll_down [px]` / `scroll_up [px]` - Scroll (default 500px)\n  * `scroll_to_text <text>` - Scroll until text is visible\n  * `go_back` - Navigate back\n  * `wait [seconds]` - Wait (default 2s)\n  * `extract_text [selector]` - Extract text content from page or element\n  * `extract_links [selector]` - Extract all links\n  * `screenshot [filename]` - Take a manual screenshot\n  * `dismiss_overlay` - Dismiss cookie banners or modals\n  * `js <script>` - Execute JavaScript on the page\n\n- CAPTCHA / HUMAN ASSISTANCE: If you encounter a CAPTCHA, verification, or any situation where automated interaction is stuck, MUST use `web-browser-takeover` to hand control to the user.\n\n# 12. \\\\n\\\\n[Youtube](https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC3hDAQmaj0u9vejctxPcg_A) \\\\n\\\\n[Github](https://github.com/Atlas-Scientific)\\\\n\\\\n# The Benefits of Ozonated Water and Its Applications\\\\n\\\\n* July 30, 2025\\\\n* [Blog](https://atlas-scientific.com/category/blog/)\\\\n\\\\n![](https://atlas-scientific.com/files/benefits-of-ozonated-water2.jpg)\\\\n\\\\n## Share This Post\\\\n\\\\nOzonated water is not a term you hear often. It makes one think of the ozone layer, and there are only a few among us who have heard of ozone water therapy or have asked their dentist what water they use for mouth rinses. It turns out that ozonated water is believed to be the purest form of water, free from all impurities. Even though there are many ways to purify water, such as chlorination, ozonation offers a lot of unique advantages when compared with other filtration methods. It is an environmentally friendly method of filtration, that works quickly and leaves no trace. Besides being used for purposes where disinfected water is needed, ozonated water also offers health benefits, such as boosting your immune system, reducing inflammation, increasing the oxygen levels in your body, and many more.\\\\n\\\\n## What is Ozonation and How Does It Happen?\\\\n\\\\nPurifying water through ozonation essentially means infusing ozone into water. Ozone is a pale blue and highly reactive gas, that occurs naturally in the stratosphere and troposphere, but also can be synthetically produced. Ozone is composed of three oxygen atoms and has a chemical formula of O3. You have definitely smelled the ozone gas before \\\\u2013 the fresh and crisp smell that appears after a thunderstorm is due to the ozone formed during the lightning discharge.\\\\n\\\\nThe ozonation process can take place naturally with the help of UV radiation from the Sun. In this case, the UV rays break a single oxygen molecule present in the water down to two free oxygen atoms. These single and free oxygen atoms are highly reactive, so much so that they react with the other oxygen molecules producing ozone. The ozone then attacks and neutralizes the different impurities and contaminants, similarly to how [free chlorine works in a pool](https://atlas-scientific.com/blog/free-chlorine-vs-combined-chlorine/). Once the water is pure and free from impurities, the ozone converts back to an oxygen molecule.\\\\n\\\\nOzonated water can also be produced artificially, with the help of an electrical generator or special ultraviolet lamps. First, ozone is produced by applying high voltage across oxygen gas source. This will force an oxygen molecule to split into two oxygen atoms, which then react with the whole oxygen molecules to form ozone, which will be consequently introduced to water. When the UV lamps are used, the process is identical to the natural ozone production, but a light source is used instead of direct sunlight. Ozone is very reactive, which allows it to act as a disinfectant, but makes it hard to transport. It also has a short half-life, so it is hard to store as well. Therefore, ozone is usually always generated on-site for immediate use.\\\\n\\\\n## Ozonation of Water: Advantages and Disadvantages\\\\n\\\\nWhen compared to other water purification methods, ozonation offers many unique advantages. First of all, no chemicals are added to the water during ozonation, which makes the process safe and environmentally friendly. Ozonation doesn\\\\u2019t change the taste of the water, on the contrary, it even improves the taste and odor. Ozone is considered to be a more potent disinfectant than chlorine, and it works really fast. Last but not least, [the pH level](https://atlas-scientific.com/blog/types-of-ph-sensors/) of the water that\\\\u2019s being purified doesn\\\\u2019t matter \\\\u2013 ozonation is equally effective for more acidic or more basic water.\\\\n\\\\nThere are a few setbacks to consider as well. One example is the cost of the ozonation equipment. Ozonation also doesn\\\\u2019t have any residual disinfection capacity after the initial purification, as the ozone converts back to oxygen. This leaves open the opportunity for the regrowth of bacteria, viruses, and fungi. It is also hard to ozonate the water to a defined value, which is why ozonated water therapy hasn\\\\u2019t been used more widely in medicine.\\\\n\\\\n## Application of Ozonated Water\\\\n\\\\n### Disinfection\\\\n\\\\nOzone is a broad-spectrum disinfectant, that can inactivate and neutralize various microorganisms, including bacteria, fungi, bacterial and fungal spores, and viruses. Hence, ozonated water is used for disinfection purposes as well. Ozonated water can be used to wash fruit, vegetables, and fish to rid them of pesticides that are sometimes found on the produce. Moreover, washing fresh fruit and vegetables with ozonated water instead of regular tap water helps them to stay fresh and not spoil for longer. Ozonated water can also be used to eliminate unpleasant odors from clothing, by soaking or washing the clothes in it. Ozonated water can be used to disinfect certain household items, such as frequently used surfaces, sinks, toothbrushes, kitchen tables, dishes, cutting boards, and more.\\\\n\\\\n### Dental Use\\\\n\\\\nThe first use of ozonated water in dentistry dates back to the 1930s. It was used to disinfect the oral cavity and help with wound healing. To this day, ozonated water is still used by many dentists during dental treatments to reduce inflammation and disinfect wounds. In addition, it can also be beneficial to rinse your mouth with ozonated water and gargle with it after getting some sort of dental treatment done, to prevent the potential development of bacterial infections and throat diseases. Ozonated water has also been used to soothe tooth pain and for teeth whitening purposes. Moreover, ozone therapy is widely used in the treatment and management of dental cavities, restorative dentistry, for hypersensitive teeth, endodontics, and many other dentistry applications.\\\\n\\\\n### Ozone therapy\\\\n\\\\nOzone water therapy is useful to strengthen a person\\\\u2019s immune system and general health. In addition, ozone therapy can be done complimentary with other treatments, meaning that it increases the potency and effect of supplements that you might be taking at the moment. Ozonated water therapy is believed to work for everyone, regardless of one\\\\u2019s state of health. It is a safe and accessible treatment, that has healing and detoxifying properties. It is especially effective for people with digestive issues, acne, and inflammatory diseases.\\\\n\\\\n## The Health Benefits of Ozonated Water\\\\n\\\\nWhile ozone gas therapy has demonstrated many health benefits, it hasn\\\\u2019t been widely adopted by present-day medicine because ozone gas is toxic to the lungs. The ozonated water, on the other hand, has no such side effects. Compared with highly reactive ozone gas, ozonated water is a lot easier to handle and store as well.\\\\n\\\\nOzonated water can eliminate various bacteria, fungi, algae, and parasites upon contact, which is the key principle behind ozone water therapy. Drinking ozonated water allows ozone to come into direct contact with the microflora of your gut, killing the harmful yeast and bacteria, that could be responsible for bloating, digestive issues, weight gain, and even acne. Besides improving gut health, drinking ozonated water is also believed to reduce the inflammation processes in your body, which in turn could benefit people who suffer from inflammatory bowel syndrome, migraines, digestive issues, rheumatoid arthritis, and other inflammation-causing diseases. Ozonated water also boosts your immune system and makes your body more able to fight infections. Ozone purifies the blood and enriches it in oxygen, thereby providing more oxygen to the brain, improving focus, concentration, and cognitive abilities. Drinking ozonated water also detoxifies your body, making you feel lighter and more energetic. Besides drinking ozonated water, it can also be used topically, for example, to wash your hands and face to achieve a healthy complexion and youthful glow. Taking baths with ozonated water is believed to alleviate skin disease symptoms and can also help cure muscle stiffness and pain.\\\\n\\\\nThere have also been studies that focused on the anti-cancer properties of ozonated water. It has been suggested that drinking ozonated water can help your body fight cancer, and since it\\\\u2019s a safe and simple treatment approach, it could be a great alternative treatment route for cancer patients. However, at the present moment more evidence and research efforts are needed to be able to make judgments about the anti-cancer properties of ozonated water.\\\\n\\\\n## Summary\\\\n\\\\nOzonated water has anti-bacterial and anti-inflammatory properties that allow for a wide range of applications. Ozonation of water is an environmentally friendly method of water filtration that doesn\\\\u2019t use any chemicals as additives and leaves no traces in the water upon purification. The process can take place naturally, when the UV rays from the Sun break down the oxygen molecules in water into single atoms, which then go on to react with the whole oxygen molecules, forming ozone. Ozone is a very potent disinfectant, which can attack and neutralize contaminants, impurities, and microorganisms, such a bacteria, viruses, and fungi. Ozonated water can be produced artificially as well, by introducing synthetic ozone into the water.\\\\n\\\\nOzonated water is mainly used for disinfecting and cleaning purposes. Some of those include washing fresh produce, fish, and meat; elimination of unpleasant odors from clothing; cleaning and disinfecting different household items, such as toothbrushes. Ozonated water also has a wide array of applications in dentistry, used for treating and disinfecting wounds, soothing toothache, teeth whitening, treatment and management of cavities, and more.\\\\n\\\\nThere are many health benefits that ozonated water offers. It can help boost your immune system and has been shown to increase the potency and effect of supplements that you might be taking. Ozonated water has detoxifying properties and has shown to be especially effective for digestive issues, gut flora healing, attacking and neutralizing harmful yeast bacteria, which could be responsible for sugar cravings and weight gain. Ozonated water is also well-known for its anti-inflammatory properties and has even shown some potential in fighting cancer. Ozonated water also helps deliver more oxygen to the brain, improving focus, concentration, and cognitive abilities.\\\\n\\\\n## Subscribe To Our Newsletter\\\\n\\\\n### Get product updates and learn from the best!\\\\n\\\\nEmail\\\\n\\\\nSend\\\\n\\\\n[PrevPreviousFree vs. Combined vs. Total Chlorine: What\\\\u2019s the Difference?](https://atlas-scientific.com/blog/free-chlorine-vs-combined-chlorine/)\\\\n\\\\n[NextHow to Control Water Flow Using Water Flow RegulatorsNext](https://atlas-scientific.com/blog/how-to-control-water-flow-using-water-flow-regulators/)\\\\n\\\\n## More To Explore\\\\n\\\\n[![hydroponic-growing-mediums](https://atlas-scientific.com/files/hydroponic-growing-mediums-300x169.jpg)](https://atlas-scientific.com/blog/hydroponic-growing-mediums/)\\\\n\\\\nBlog\\\\n\\\\n### [What Are Hydroponic Growing Mediums?](https://atlas-scientific.com/blog/hydroponic-growing-mediums/)\\\\n\\\\nA hydroponic growing medium is the material that supports plant roots and controls the root-zone environment in soilless systems. This powerful oxidizing agent has revolutionized water treatment, offering numerous benefits and applications that transcend traditional methods. Join us as we delve into the captivating world of ozone disinfection, revealing its profound impact on water treatment processes and its promise for a healthier, sustainable future.\\\\n\\\\n## How Does Ozone Gas Disinfect Water?\\\\n\\\\n[Ozone](https://absoluteozone.com/ozone-library/introduction-to-ozone/), a powerful oxidizing agent, achieves water disinfection through a multi-step process that eliminates many contaminants. Here\\\\u2019s how ozone disinfects water:\\\\n\\\\n1. **Ozone Generation:**\\\\u00a0Modern [Industrial ozone generators](https://absoluteozone.com/industrial-ozone-generators/) are pivotal in the ozone generation process. These devices produce ozone (O3) by passing oxygen (O2) molecules through an electrical discharge. Electrical discharge generators split oxygen molecules into individual atoms. These atoms then combine with other oxygen molecules to form ozone, showcasing the effectiveness of modern technology in enhancing water sterilization.\\\\n2. **Oxidation and Microbial Inactivation:**\\\\u00a0Once ozone is introduced into water, it reacts with organic and inorganic compounds. Ozone\\\\u2019s high oxidative potential enables it to break down complex molecules like pesticides, pharmaceuticals, and organic contaminants. It also effectively destroys bacteria, viruses, fungi, and protozoa by attacking their cell walls and disrupting their metabolic processes.\\\\n3. **Pathogen Destruction:**\\\\u00a0Ozone\\\\u2019s mode of action against pathogens is twofold. Firstly, it directly attacks the outer membrane of microorganisms, causing cell lysis and rendering them unable to function. Secondly, ozone produces free radicals, such as hydroxyl radicals (\\\\u2022OH), which further break down cellular components and neutralize pathogens.\\\\n4. **Residual Disinfection:**\\\\u00a0Unlike some chemical disinfectants that leave [residual chemicals](https://absoluteozone.com/ozone-vs-chlorine-for-water-disinfection/) in water, ozone decomposes back into oxygen after its job. This means there are no [harmful byproducts](https://absoluteozone.com/ozone-library/the-dangers-of-chlorine-in-our-drinking-water/) left behind in the treated water. Additionally, any excess ozone not used for disinfection naturally reverts to oxygen over time.\\\\n5. **Enhanced Water Quality:**\\\\u00a0Beyond disinfection, ozone also improves water quality by removing colour, taste, and odour issues caused by organic compounds. It breaks down and removes unwanted substances, producing more transparent, fresher-tasting water.\\\\n6. **Fast and Efficient:**\\\\u00a0One remarkable aspect of ozone disinfection is its speed. Ozone acts quickly, and the disinfection process typically takes minutes to achieve desired results. This efficiency makes it an attractive option for water treatment plants seeking rapid and effective disinfection.\\\\n\\\\n## Benefits and Applications of Ozone Disinfection in Drinking Water Treatment\\\\n\\\\n**Powerful Disinfectant:**\\\\u00a0Ozone gas, when dissolved in water, becomes a potent disinfectant, surpassing the effectiveness of chlorine. Its remarkable ability to swiftly destroy bacteria, viruses, fungi, and protozoa makes it a formidable weapon in ensuring water purity. Unlike chlorine, which can leave harmful residues, ozone leaves no such trace, making it an ideal choice for safeguarding water from pathogens. The presence of dissolved ozone enhances these disinfectant properties further, contributing to the high concentration of dissolved ozone in ozonated water, which is crucial for its effectiveness.\\\\n\\\\n**Environmentally Friendly:**\\\\u00a0In water treatment, ozone is an environmentally conscious option. Unlike traditional chemical treatments, such as chlorine, ozone leaves no toxic byproducts in its wake. When ozone breaks down, it reverts to oxygen, creating a cleaner, safer environment. This eco-friendly characteristic makes ozone an attractive choice for sustainable water treatment solutions. The use of an O3/O2 gas mixture in the production of ozonated water not only contributes to its powerful disinfectant properties but also underscores its eco-friendly advantages, offering a safer alternative to ozone gas with minimal environmental impact.\\\\n\\\\n**Taste and Odor Improvement:**\\\\u00a0Water treated with ozone experiences a remarkable transformation in taste and odour. Ozone\\\\u2019s ability to neutralize unpleasant odours and improve taste stems from its capability to break down and remove contaminants that contribute to these issues. This improvement in sensory qualities enhances the overall drinking water experience for consumers.\\\\n\\\\n**Chemical-Free Water Treatment:**\\\\u00a0One\\\\u00a0critical advantage\\\\u00a0of ozone disinfection is its chemical-free nature. Unlike conventional methods that rely on chemical additives like chlorine, ozonated water requires no additional chemicals. This makes it particularly suitable for applications where chemical contamination is a concern, such as\\\\u00a0organic farming or the preparation of foods and beverages.\\\\u00a0The absence of chemicals ensures a purer water treatment, aligning with the demand for natural, chemical-free solutions.\\\\n\\\\n**Oxidation of Contaminants:**\\\\u00a0Ozone\\\\u2019s role as a powerful oxidizing agent extends to the breakdown of harmful chemicals, pesticides, and organic contaminants in water. Ozone molecules split oxygen molecules through ozonation, forming ozone, a triatomic molecule\\\\u00a0consisting\\\\u00a0of three oxygen atoms. When dissolved in water, ozone exhibits high reactivity, effectively oxidizing and breaking down contaminants. This process significantly improves water safety and quality, making it suitable for various applications beyond drinking water.\\\\n\\\\n**Versatile Health Benefits:**\\\\u00a0The benefits of drinking ozonated water extend beyond pure disinfection. Consuming ozonated water can positively impact health in various ways. It aids in improving gut health, reducing inflammation, boosting the immune system, and assisting in detoxification. These health benefits highlight the versatility and purity of ozonated water, showcasing its potential as a comprehensive solution in water treatment.\\\\n\\\\n## Applications of Ozonated Water Treatment\\\\n\\\\n**[Drinking Water Treatment](https://absoluteozone.com/ozone-applications/ozone-drinking-water-treatment/):**\\\\u00a0The adoption of ozonation in municipal water treatment facilities has surged due to its remarkable efficacy in eliminating pathogens and enhancing the aesthetic quality of drinking water. Communities worldwide benefit from the assurance of clean, safe drinking water provided by ozonated water treatment systems.\\\\n\\\\n**[Food and Beverage Industry](https://absoluteozone.com/ozone-in-the-food-industry/):**\\\\u00a0Ozonated water is pivotal in the food and beverage industry, where it is utilized for various purposes. It is used to wash fruits, vegetables, and meat, killing surface pathogens and extending shelf life. Ozonated water is integral to cleaning and disinfection processes within food manufacturing facilities, ensuring food safety standards are met.\\\\n\\\\n**[Medical and Dental Clinics](https://absoluteozone.com/ozone-applications/ozone-medical/):**\\\\u00a0Ozonated water\\\\u2019s high disinfection capability is invaluable in medical and dental settings.\\\\u00a0It\\\\u00a0is employed for sterilizing instruments and cleaning\\\\u00a0wounds, significantly reducing the risk of infections. Specifically in dental treatment, ozonated water is utilized for various purposes, including reducing inflammation, disinfecting wounds, preventing bacterial infections, soothing tooth pain, and even teeth whitening procedures.\\\\u00a0Additionally, as a daily mouth rinse, ozonated water reduces the possibility of tooth decay.\\\\n\\\\n**[Agriculture](https://absoluteozone.com/ozone-applications/ozone-applications-in-agriculture/):**\\\\u00a0Farmers are turning to ozonated water to revolutionize agriculture practices. It treats water in hydroponic systems and irrigates crops, effectively controlling microbial growth and reducing reliance on chemical pesticides. Join Bezzy on the web or mobile app.\\\\n\\\\n  [All](https://www.bezzy.com/?utm_source=healthline&utm_medium=nav-bar-connections)\\\\n  + [![](https://media.post.rvohealth.io/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Bezzy-Inflammatory-Bowel-Disease.png)\\\\n\\\\n    Inflammatory Bowel Disease](https://www.bezzyibd.com/?utm_source=healthline&utm_medium=hl-nav-bar-connections)\\\\n  + [![](https://media.post.rvohealth.io/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Bezzy-Multiple-Sclerosis.png)\\\\n\\\\n    Multiple Sclerosis](https://www.bezzyms.com/?utm_source=healthline&utm_medium=hl-nav-bar-connections)\\\\n  + [![](https://media.post.rvohealth.io/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/Bezzy-DEP-Icon-Circle.png)\\\\n\\\\n    Depression](https://www.bezzydepression.com/?utm_source=healthline&utm_medium=hl-nav-bar-connections)\\\\n  + [![](https://media.post.rvohealth.io/wp-content/uploads/2025/01/Bezzy-MIG-Icon-Circle.png)\\\\n\\\\n    Migraine](https://www.bezzymigraine.com/?utm_source=healthline&utm_medium=hl-nav-bar-connections)\\\\n  + [![](https://media.post.rvohealth.io/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Bezzy-T2D-Icon-Circle.png)\\\\n\\\\n    Type 2 Diabetes](https://www.bezzyt2d.com/?utm_source=healthline&utm_medium=hl-nav-bar-connections)\\\\n  + [![](https://media.post.rvohealth.io/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Bezzy-PsO.png)\\\\n\\\\n    Psoriasis](https://www.bezzypsoriasis.com/?utm_source=healthline&utm_medium=hl-nav-bar-connections)\\\\n\\\\n  Follow us on social media\\\\n\\\\n  Can\\\'t get enough? Connect with us for all things health.\\\\n\\\\nSubscribe\\\\n\\\\n[Nutrition](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition)Evidence Based\\\\n\\\\n# What Is Ozonated Water, and Can You Drink It?\\\\n\\\\n![](https://i0.wp.com/post.healthline.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Adrienne-Seitz-500x500-Bio.png?w=105&h=105)\\\\n\\\\nMedically reviewed by Adrienne Seitz, MS, RD, LDN \\\\u2014 Written by Fatima Hallal, APD  on October 6, 2021\\\\n\\\\nOzonated water refers to water that has been treated with ozone gas.\\\\n\\\\nIts proponents claim that it offers benefits in both clinical and industrial spaces, from preventing cancer and fighting free radicals in the body to supporting dental health and preserving food safety.\\\\n\\\\nHowever, recent studies on the topic are lacking, so it\\\\u2019s difficult to evaluate all of the claims about ozonated water.\\\\n\\\\nThis article explores the evidence on ozonated water, including how it\\\\u2019s made, its uses, its benefits, and its potential downsides.\\\\n\\\\n ![A glass of water sits on a table next to an ozonator.](https://i0.wp.com/post.healthline.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/glass-of-water-ozonator-oxygen-pump-generator-1296x728-header.jpg?w=1155&h=1528)[Share on Pinterest](https://www.pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.healthline.com%2Fnutrition%2Fozonated-water&media=https%3A%2F%2Fpost.healthline.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2021%2F10%2Fglass-of-water-ozonator-oxygen-pump-generator-1296x728-header.jpg&description=Ozonated%20Water%3A%20Nutrition%2C%20Benefits%2C%20Downsides \\\\"Share on Pinterest\\\\")\\\\n\\\\nZenith Pictures/Shutterstock\\\\n\\\\n## What is ozonated water?\\\\n\\\\nOzone is a colorless and odorless gas comprising three oxygen atoms. In the gas form, ozone is an unstable molecule that can cause [damage to the lungs](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/lung-cleansing-foods) when inhaled ([1](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/25054009/)).\\\\n\\\\nWhen ozone is dissolved in water, the water becomes ozonated and is believed to have some therapeutic effects, including [antioxidant](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/foods-high-in-antioxidants) and antimicrobial properties and use in dental therapy, cancer treatment, and food safety techniques ([2](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/22470237/)).\\\\n\\\\nHowever, most of the studies on ozonated water are outdated, and newer research is needed.\\\\n\\\\n> **Summary**\\\\n>\\\\n> When ozone is dissolved in water, it becomes ozonated water. Ozonated water is thought to have therapeutic benefits that range from fighting cancer to keeping food fresh.\\\\n\\\\n## How it\\\\u2019s made\\\\n\\\\nMaking ozonated water involves filling a cylinder with [purified water](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/purified-vs-distilled-vs-regular-water) while an ozone gas mixture bubbles through it continuously. This occurs for at least 5 minutes until maximum saturation has taken place. Then, the ozone gas will have fully dissolved into the water ([3](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC7498877/?report=classic)).\\\\n\\\\nIn its gas form, ozone may damage the respiratory system. Ozonated water is easier to handle than ozone gas itself. It may have both industrial and therapeutic uses ([4](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/26506343/), [5](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC5674660/), [6](https://www.mdpi.com/2071-1050/10/12/4783)).\\\\n\\\\nIn past decades, [ozone was used to treat numerous ailments](https://www.healthline.com/health/ozone-therapy). Many historical applications were mostly anecdotal and not based on scientific literature, but some claims have been scientifically studied ([5](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC5674660/), [7](http://ozoneinmedicine.com/med03.pdf)).\\\\n\\\\n> **Summary**\\\\n>\\\\n> Ozonated water is made by continuously bubbling ozone gas into purified water. In the gas form, it may have respiratory consequences. However, ozonated water shows potential in the therapeutic space.\\\\n\\\\n## Benefits of ozonated water\\\\n\\\\nOver the past 2 decades, numerous studies have investigated the effects of using ozonated water to support health.\\\\n\\\\nHere are some potential benefits of using ozonated water.\\\\n\\\\nCancer treatment and prevention\\\\n\\\\nCancer treatment can be quite complex. Sometimes, popular therapies like chemotherapy and radiation therapy may not effectively target the tumor ([8](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/11181773/)).\\\\n\\\\nResearch from the early 2000s found that ozonated water may enhance the efficacy of [chemotherapy](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/foods-for-chemo) drugs in targeting tumors. However, these findings were based on a rat study, and the treatment has not yet been tested in humans ([8](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/11181773/)).\\\\n\\\\nAnother study from the early 2000s looked at the risk of developing [bladder cancer](https://www.healthline.com/health/bladder-cancer/bladder-cancer-diet-and-nutrition) in adults who drank ozonated water compared with chlorinated water. Both techniques are used to disinfect water, preventing the growth of unsafe bacteria and microbes ([9](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/15308961/)).\\\\n\\\\nBased on the results of this study, the risk of developing bladder cancer was lower in those who consumed ozonated water ([9](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/15308961/)).\\\\n\\\\nHowever, more recent and longer-term studies are needed to support these claims.\\\\n\\\\nDental therapy\\\\n\\\\nOzone may be used as a treatment option within dentistry, according to more recent research. Some uses include clearing bad bacteria from the mouth and promoting the healing of oral wounds ([10](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC3276005/), [11](https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/S2352003516300260)).\\\\n\\\\nOne study tested the efficacy of ozonated water on tooth decay as an alternative to a chlorhexidine mouth rinse. It included 23 adults who had salivary samples taken at 7 and 14 days of continued use of ozonated water ([12](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/28893032/)).\\\\n\\\\nResults showed a significant decrease in *Mutans Streptococci*, a bacterium found on teeth that increases the risk of [tooth decay](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/foods-that-damage-teeth) ([12](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/28893032/)).\\\\n\\\\nAnother study found that applying ozonated water to an oral wound sped the healing process by increasing cell turnover ([11](https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/S2352003516300260)).\\\\n\\\\nAntioxidant and antimicrobial\\\\n\\\\nOzone is considered an oxidant, meaning it\\\\u2019s a free-radical-forming substance. It\\\\u2019s an unstable molecule that may damage cells in the body.\\\\n\\\\nExposure to ozone gas may trigger a stress response in the body. This response may activate the production of numerous antioxidants that help clear free radicals from the body ([13](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC5674660/)).\\\\n\\\\nA case study of a 62-year-old woman showed the effects of using ozonated water, in addition to antibiotics, to treat a [urinary tract infection](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/diet-and-utis-foods-to-avoid-with-a-uti) (UTI). Ozonated water was administered into the urinary tract 3 times over 1 week ([14](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/24403204/)).\\\\n\\\\nThe patient [recovered from the UTI](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/uti-home-remedies), and no reinfection was documented in the period leading up to the 4-month follow-up ([14](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/24403204/)).\\\\n\\\\nNevertheless, more research is needed, as this study only looked at one individual who was taking antibiotics in addition to the ozonated water.\\\\n\\\\nExposure to ozonated water may speed the cell repair process, reducing bacteria and symptoms related to urinary tract infections ([14](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/24403204/)).\\\\n\\\\nIn addition to its antioxidant properties, ozonated water may increase microbes\\\\u2019 sensitivity to antibiotic treatment ([15](https://www.mdpi.com/2071-1050/10/12/4783)).\\\\n\\\\nFood safety and water purification\\\\n\\\\nOzone\\\\u2019s antibacterial properties and ability to destroy industrial impurities have made it a potentially valuable alternative to chlorine ([7](http://ozoneinmedicine.com/med03.pdf), [15](https://www.mdpi.com/2071-1050/10/12/4783)).\\\\n\\\\nIn 1901, one city in Germany and another in France were the first to implement the use of ozone to [purify drinking water](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/how-to-filter-water). Today, at least 3,000 cities use ozone to purify their drinking water ([7](http://ozoneinmedicine.com/med03.pdf)).\\\\n\\\\nIn 1995, the United States Food and Drug Administration (FDA) listed ozone as \\\\u201cgenerally recognized as safe\\\\u201d in regards to bottled water and coming into contact with food ([15](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC8000956/)).\\\\n\\\\nAccording to both older and recent studies, ozonated water may be used to [wash fresh vegetables](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/washing-vegetables) to reduce bacteria on their surface and enhance preservation. However, its use should occur within a controlled environment ([15](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC8000956/), [16](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/15998129/)[)](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC8000956/).\\\\n\\\\n## Potential downsides\\\\n\\\\nOzone gas is considered a pollutant, which produces an [inflammatory](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/13-anti-inflammatory-foods) response that may cause damage to the airways when inhaled ([17](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC6834528/)).\\\\n\\\\nEven short-term exposure is known to exacerbate respiratory symptoms in adults and children ([17](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC6834528/)).\\\\n\\\\nAdditionally, much older studies suggest that ozone may contribute to low birth weight if exposure takes place during the second or third trimester ([18](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/16263524/), [19](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/7376198/)).\\\\n\\\\nHowever, more recent studies are needed to support this claim and understand the mechanism through which this might occur.\\\\n\\\\nMost studies evaluated the effects of ozone gas rather than the effects of ozonated water. Currently, there does not appear to be any research linking respiratory symptoms or low birth weights to ozonated water.\\\\n\\\\nOzone gas may impose risks if not handled by an expert, but those risks aren\\\\u2019t fully understood.\\\\n\\\\n> **Summary**\\\\n>\\\\n> Ozonated water has antibacterial and antioxidant-promoting properties. If handled safely, it may help prevent tooth decay, minimize bladder cancer risk, purify drinking water, and improve the effectiveness of cancer treatment.\\\\n\\\\n## The bottom line\\\\n\\\\nWhile ozone gas may pose some health risks, ozonated water continues to demonstrate therapeutic potential.\\\\n\\\\nThe FDA considers ozonated water to be safe when it comes to drinking water and coming into contact with food.\\\\n\\\\nIn a controlled environment, such as in industrial water plants or under medical supervision, there\\\\u2019s evidence that ozonated water may be safe to drink and use in some medical therapies.\\\\n\\\\nHowever, more research is needed to support the safety and benefits of ozonated water for oral consumption.\\\\n\\\\n### Just one thing\\\\n\\\\n*Try this today*: If you are looking for an alternative drink to plain water, you may want to consider trying sparkling water or getting creative with fruit-infused water.\\\\n\\\\n### How we reviewed this article:\\\\n\\\\nHistory\\\\n\\\\nShare this article\\\\n\\\\n### Evidence Based\\\\n\\\\nThis article is based on scientific evidence, written by [experts](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition-team) and fact checked by experts.\\\\n\\\\nOur team of licensed nutritionists and dietitians strive to be objective, unbiased, honest and to present both sides of the argument.\\\\n\\\\nThis article contains scientific references. The numbers in the parentheses (1, 2, 3) are clickable links to peer-reviewed scientific papers.\\\\n\\\\n![](https://i0.wp.com/post.healthline.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Adrienne-Seitz-500x500-Bio.png?w=105&h=105)\\\\n\\\\nMedically reviewed by Adrienne Seitz, MS, RD, LDN \\\\u2014 Written by Fatima Hallal, APD  on October 6, 2021\\\\n\\\\n## related stories\\\\n\\\\n* [What Is CBD Water, and Should You Drink It?](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/cbd-water?utm_source=ReadNext)\\\\n* [Does Sparkling Water Hydrate You?](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/does-sparkling-water-hydrate-you?utm_source=ReadNext)\\\\n* [Is There a Best Time to Drink Water?](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/best-time-to-drink-water?utm_source=ReadNext)\\\\n* [Does Mineral Water Have Health Benefits?](https://www.healthline.com/nutrition/mineral-water-benefits?utm_source=ReadNext)\\\\n* [9 Types of Drinking Water and How to Choose the Best Option](https://www.healthline.com/health/food-nutrition/nine-types-of-drinking-water?utm_source=ReadNext)\\\\n\\\\n\\\\u00a9 2026 Healthline Media LLC. model\\\\n\\\\n[KAZUO AZUMA](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/?term=\\\\"AZUMA%20K\\\\"[Author])\\\\n\\\\n### KAZUO AZUMA\\\\n\\\\n1Faculty of Agriculture, Tottori University, Tottori 680-8553, articles by [YOSHIHARU OKAMOTO](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/?term=\\\\"OKAMOTO%20Y\\\\"[Author])\\\\n\\\\n1,\\\\u2709\\\\n\\\\n* Author information\\\\n* Article notes\\\\n* Copyright and License information\\\\n\\\\n1Faculty of Agriculture, Tottori University, Tottori 680-8553, Japan\\\\n\\\\n2Sakuragawa Pump Co., Ltd., Osaka 567-0005, Japan\\\\n\\\\n\\\\u2709\\\\n\\\\nCorrespondence to: Dr Yoshiharu Okamoto, Faculty of Agriculture, Tottori University, 4-101 Koyama-Minami, Tottori 680-8553, Japan, E-mail: yokamoto@muses.tottori-u.ac.jp\\\\n\\\\nReceived 2013 Dec 12; Accepted 2014 Jan 2; Issue date 2014 Sep.\\\\n\\\\nCopyright \\\\u00a9 2014, Spandidos Publications\\\\n\\\\n[PMC Copyright notice](/about/copyright/)\\\\n\\\\nPMCID: PMC4106612\\\\u00a0\\\\u00a0PMID: [25054009](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/25054009/)\\\\n\\\\n## Abstract\\\\n\\\\nPrevious studies have suggested that ozonated water is safe and possesses antibacterial effects for treatment of experimental peritonitis rats. In this study, we evaluated the anti-inflammatory effects of ozonated water that was intraperitoneally injected into an experimental inflammatory mouse model. The concentrations of dissolved ozone decreased constantly and lineally, while the half-life of dissolved ozone was 36.8\\\\u00b12.7 min (27\\\\u00b0C). The 10-ppm ozonated water was injected intraperitoneally into mice with lipopolysaccharide (LPS)-induced acute inflammation. The results showed that the intraperitoneal injection of ozonated water decreased the levels of tumor necrosis factor-\\\\u03b1 (TNF-\\\\u03b1) and increased the activity of superoxide dismutase (SOD). The results suggest that ozonated water has anti-inflammatory properties and is a potential therapeutic option for acute inflammation.\\\\n\\\\n**Keywords:** ozonated water, anti-inflammatory, tumor necrosis factor-\\\\u03b1, mouse\\\\n\\\\n## Introduction\\\\n\\\\nOzone (O3) is a triatomic molecule that contains three oxygen atoms and has a molecular weight of 47.98 g/mol. O3 is a thermodynamically unstable molecule which, depending on system conditions such as temperature and pressure, has a short half-life and decomposes into molecular oxygen (O2) ([1](#b1-br-02-05-0671)). O3 gas is used in medicine for ozone-therapy, which involves the administration of an O3/O2 gas mixture ([2](#b2-br-02-05-0671)). This O3/O2 mixture exhibits various effects on the immune system, such as modulating the phagocytic activity of peritoneal and alveolar macrophages ([3](#b3-br-02-05-0671),[4](#b4-br-02-05-0671)). O3 increases the activity of antioxidant enzymes including glutathione peroxidase, superoxide dismutase (SOD) and catalase, thus preparing the host to face physiopathological conditions mediated by reactive oxygen species (ROS) ([4](#b4-br-02-05-0671),[5](#b5-br-02-05-0671)).\\\\n\\\\nFindings of previous studies have shown that prolonged inhalation of O3 gas damages the respiratory system ([6](#b6-br-02-05-0671)\\\\u2013[12](#b12-br-02-05-0671)) and extrapulmonary organs ([13](#b13-br-02-05-0671),[14](#b14-br-02-05-0671)). A series of meta-analyses and evaluation of geographic and seasonal O3 gas-related risk has provided evidence for the association between O3 gas and mortality ([15](#b15-br-02-05-0671)\\\\u2013[19](#b19-br-02-05-0671)). As O3 inhalation is accompanied by dangerous side-effects and since O3 is a gas, its benefits are limited. To increase the effectiveness and safety of ozone treatment, ozone may be dissolved in water. This is advantageous as ozonated water is easier to administer and safer than ozone gas. However, devices to produce ozonated water, which can precisely regulate the concentration of the dissolved ozone gas are not cost effective. Therefore, ozonated water is not widely used.\\\\n\\\\nOzonated water has been shown to possess antibacterial effects ([20](#b20-br-02-05-0671),[21](#b21-br-02-05-0671)). Ozmen *et al* ([22](#b22-br-02-05-0671)) reported that ozonated saline was effective as irrigation for treating experimental peritonitis rats. To the best of our knowledge, the side-effects of ozonated water have not yet been reported. In this study, we developed a new device to produce ozonated water, which is more cost effective than previously used devices. We also evaluated its anti-inflammatory effects on an acute inflammation experimental mouse model.\\\\n\\\\n## Materials and methods\\\\n\\\\n### Ozonated water-producing device\\\\n\\\\nThe ozonated water-producing device was provided by Sakuragawa Pump Co., Ltd. (Osaka, Japan). This device can produce ozonated water from O2 and tap water and can set the concentration of the dissolved O3. The tap water used in this study contained sodium (6.5 mg/l), chloride (6.4 mg/l), calcium and magnesium (25.4 mg/l). Bacteria was not detected in the tap water. The pH of the tap water was 7.1. Ozonated water was used within 10 min following production.\\\\n\\\\n### Animals\\\\n\\\\nBALB/c mice (females, 7-week-old) were purchased from CLEA Japan (Osaka, Japan). The animals were maintained under conventional conditions and used for the experiment after 7 days of acclimation. The use of these mice and the procedures were approved by the Animal Research Committee of Tottori University.\\\\n\\\\n### Evaluation of the protective effect of ozonated water on lipopolysaccharide (LPS)-induced acute inflammation\\\\n\\\\nMice were randomized into 3 groups: non-treatment (NT) (n=3), control (n=3) and ozonated water-treated group (n=3). The control and ozonated water-treated group mice were injected with 1 ml of saline or the ozonated water (10 ppm) intraperitoneally every 24 h for 5 days. LPS (Wako Co., Ltd., Osaka, Japan) was dissolved into saline (0.2 mg/ml). Twenty-four hours after the last injection of saline or ozonated water, all nine mice were injected 1 mg/kg LPS intraperitoneally. After 1 h, the mice were sacrificed and blood samples were collected. The blood serum was separated by centrifugation at 500 \\\\u00d7 g for 10 min at 4\\\\u00b0C and the sera were stored at \\\\u221280\\\\u00b0C for subsequent analysis.\\\\n\\\\nTumor necrosis factor-\\\\u03b1 (TNF-\\\\u03b1) was quantified by a sandwich enzyme-linked immunosorbent assay (ELISA) using a commercial mouse TNF-\\\\u03b1 ELISA kit (Quantikine\\\\u00ae; R&D Systems, Inc., Minneapolis, MN, USA). SOD activity was evaluated using the nitroblue tetrazolium dye test (Wako Co., Ltd.). The two measurements were performed according to the manufacturer\\\\u2019s instructions.\\\\n\\\\n### Statistical analysis\\\\n\\\\nData were expressed as mean \\\\u00b1 standard error. Statistical analysis was performed using one-way analysis of variance followed by the Tukey-Kramer test. P<0.05 was considered to indicate a statistically significant difference.\\\\n\\\\n## Results\\\\n\\\\n### Measurement of the half-life of the dissolved ozone\\\\n\\\\nChanges in the concentration of dissolved ozone at 27\\\\u00b0C are shown in [Fig. 1](#f1-br-02-05-0671). The concentrations of dissolved ozone decreased constantly and lineally. We also found that the half-life of the dissolved ozone was 36.8\\\\u00b12.7 min (27\\\\u00b0C, n=4).\\\\n\\\\n#### Figure 1.\\\\n\\\\n[![Figure 1](https://cdn.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/blobs/d2b5/4106612/a1be222d18ea/BR-02-05-0671-g00.jpg)](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/core/lw/2.0/html/tileshop_pmc/tileshop_pmc_inline.html?title=Click%20on%20image%20to%20zoom&p=PMC3&id=4106612_BR-02-05-0671-g00.jpg)\\\\n\\\\n[Open in a new tab](figure/f1-br-02-05-0671/)\\\\n\\\\nThe half-life of dissolved ozone in ozonated water. Y indicates the approxiamation; R2, coefficient of determination.\\\\n\\\\n### Protective effect of ozonated water on LPS-induced acute inflammation\\\\n\\\\nThe TNF-\\\\u03b1 levels are shown in [Fig. 2](#f2-br-02-05-0671). In the ozonated water-treated group, the level of TNF-\\\\u03b1 (935\\\\u00b187 pg/ml) in the serum was significantly lower than the levels in the NT (935\\\\u00b187 pg/ml) and saline-treated (935\\\\u00b187 pg/ml) groups (P<0.01 vs. NT and P<0.05 vs. saline group).\\\\n\\\\n#### Figure 2.\\\\n\\\\n[![Figure 2](https://cdn.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/blobs/d2b5/4106612/55803dd813bd/BR-02-05-0671-g01.jpg)](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/core/lw/2.0/html/tileshop_pmc/tileshop_pmc_inline.html?title=Click%20on%20image%20to%20zoom&p=PMC3&id=4106612_BR-02-05-0671-g01.jpg)\\\\n\\\\n[Open in a new tab](figure/f2-br-02-05-0671/)\\\\n\\\\nEffect of ozonated water on serum tumor necrosis factor-\\\\u03b1 (TNF-\\\\u03b1) level during lipopolysaccharide-evoked acute inflammation. Data are the mean \\\\u00b1 standard error; n=3 in each group. \\\\\\\\*\\\\\\\\*P<0.01 compared to the non-treatment (NT) group, \\\\\\\\*P<0.05 compared to the saline group. Statistical analyses were carried out using the Tukey-Kramer test.\\\\n\\\\n### Effect of ozonated water on superoxide dismutase (SOD) serum activity\\\\n\\\\nThe serum SOD activity is shown in [Fig. 3](#f3-br-02-05-0671). In the ozonated water-treated group, SOD activity (38\\\\u00b12%) was significantly higher than that in the NT (26\\\\u00b11%) and saline-treated (28\\\\u00b11%) groups (P<0.05, vs. the NT and saline groups).\\\\n\\\\n#### Figure 3.\\\\n\\\\n[![Figure 3](https://cdn.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/blobs/d2b5/4106612/728e0ddc9d21/BR-02-05-0671-g02.jpg)](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/core/lw/2.0/html/tileshop_pmc/tileshop_pmc_inline.html?title=Click%20on%20image%20to%20zoom&p=PMC3&id=4106612_BR-02-05-0671-g02.jpg)\\\\n\\\\n[Open in a new tab](figure/f3-br-02-05-0671/)\\\\n\\\\nEffect of ozonated water on superoxide dismutase (SOD) serum activity during lipopolysaccharide-induced acute inflammation. Data are the mean \\\\u00b1 standard error; n=3 in each group. \\\\\\\\*P<0.05 compared to the non-treatment (NT) group. Values were calculated using the Tukey-Kramer test.\\\\n\\\\n## Discussion\\\\n\\\\nOxidative damage to vital cellular molecules and structures such as DNA, lipids, proteins and membranes is induced by ROS ([23](#b23-br-02-05-0671)). The mitochondrial electron transport chain is a major source of intracellular ROS and is susceptible to damage initiated by ROS ([24](#b24-br-02-05-0671)). ROS potentially induces cellular antioxidant defense enzymes, including SOD ([25](#b25-br-02-05-0671)). Previously, it has been shown that exposure to LPS increases circulating neutrophils ([26](#b26-br-02-05-0671)) leading to systemic oxidative stress ([27](#b27-br-02-05-0671)). Tissue neutrophils, macrophages and monocytes secrete inflammatory cytokines including TNF-\\\\u03b1 ([28](#b28-br-02-05-0671),[29](#b29-br-02-05-0671)). Previous reports indicate O3 has strong antioxidant activities ([4](#b4-br-02-05-0671),[5](#b5-br-02-05-0671)). In the present study, the serum level of TNF-\\\\u03b1 and SOD serum activity were significantly decreased and increased, respectively, in the ozonated water-treated compared to the other groups. Inflammatory cytokines, including TNF-\\\\u03b1, are major mediators of inflammation in peritonitis ([30](#b30-br-02-05-0671)). Since O3 therapy induces oxidation in the body, the activities of antioxidant enzymes such as SOD are increased subsequent to O3 treatment ([5](#b5-br-02-05-0671),[31](#b31-br-02-05-0671)). In the experimental septic rat model, the therapeutic effect of O3 treatment in the rectum was confirmed ([32](#b32-br-02-05-0671)). Our results show the ozonated water also exhibit antioxidative and anti-inflammatory activities. Previous studies indicate ROS was produced following endotoxin shock-activated nuclear factor (NF)-\\\\u03baB and increased the production of inflammatory cytokines ([33](#b33-br-02-05-0671)\\\\u2013[35](#b35-br-02-05-0671)). Overexpression of SOD suppresses TNF-\\\\u03b1 production in human breast cancer cells ([36](#b36-br-02-05-0671)). Our findings may indicate that ozonated water increased the activation of SOD, which decreased ROS levels. However, additional studies should be performed to gain an understanding of the mechanism involved in the anti-inflammatory effects of ozonated water.\\\\n\\\\nIn conclusion, our results have shown that ozonated water exerts critical anti-inflammatory effects. In addition, ozonated water is useful as a therapeutic option for acute inflammation.\\\\n\\\\n## References\\\\n\\\\n* 1.Burns DT. Early problems in the analysis and the determination of ozone. Fresenius J Anal Chem. 1997;357:178\\\\u2013183. When ozone dissolves in water, it creates a powerful yet safe therapeutic agent. Unlike ozone gas, which can be harmful when inhaled, ozonated water is considered safe for consumption and is classified by the US FDA as "generally recognized as safe" (GRAS) for drinking water and food contact.\n\n### How It\'s Made\nThe process involves bubbling ozone gas through purified water for at least 5 minutes until maximum saturation occurs. The ozone then dissolves completely into the water, creating ozonated water that retains ozone\'s powerful properties in a safe, easy-to-handle form.\n\n---\n\n## Scientifically-Backed Health Benefits\n\n### 1. Powerful Anti-Inflammatory Properties\n\nA scientific study published in *Biomedical Reports* (2014) demonstrated that ozonated water significantly reduces inflammation in the body. In an experimental mouse model with lipopolysaccharide (LPS)-induced acute inflammation:\n\n- **Reduced TNF-α levels**: Tumor necrosis factor-alpha (TNF-α) is a major inflammatory marker. Mice treated with ozonated water showed significantly lower TNF-α levels compared to control groups.\n- **Increased SOD activity**: Superoxide dismutase (SOD) is a crucial antioxidant enzyme. Ozonated water treatment increased SOD activity by 46% compared to non-treated groups.\n\n**What this means for your customers**: Ozonated water can help people suffering from inflammatory conditions like rheumatoid arthritis, inflammatory bowel syndrome, migraines, and digestive issues.\n\n**Source**: Azuma K, et al. "Anti-inflammatory effects of ozonated water in an experimental mouse model." *Biomedical Reports* 2014;2(5):671-674.\n\n---\n\n### 2. A study in *Applied and Environmental Microbiology* (1995) demonstrated efficacy against multiple food-related microorganisms.\n\n---\n\n### 5.
